  In the third year, she invited double the number from the previous year, so she invited 4X people.
  Similarly, in the fourth year, she invited 8X people, in the fifth year, she invited 16X people, and so on.
  Each term in the sequence is obtained by multiplying the previous term by 2.
  Therefore, it is an exponential function where each term is twice the previous term.
  Specifically, $f(n) = 30 \cdot 2^{n-1}$ where n is the number of years after the first year.
  Therefore, the function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.
  The answer is D: The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.

Question: Survey Results\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|}\hlineAnswer & Percent \\\hlineNever & $31.3 \%$ \\\hlineRarely & $24.3 \%$ \\\hlineOften & $13.5 \%$ \\\hlineAlways & $30.9 \%$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows the results of a survey in which tablet users were asked how often they would watch video advertisements in order to access streaming content for free. Based on the table, which of the following is closest to the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never"?
Choices:
  A: 0.31
  B: 0.38
  C: 0.45
  D: 0.69
Response 0:
Thought: 
    Probability of answering "Always" given not answering "Never" is the probability of answering "Always" divided by the sum of the probabilities of answering "Rarely," "Often," and "Always."
    The probability of answering "Always" is $30.9\%$, and the probability of not answering "Never" is $100\% - 31.3\% = 68.7\%$.
    The sum of the probabilities of answering "Rarely," "Often," and "Always" is $24.3\% + 13.5\% + 30.9\% = 68.7\%$.
    Therefore, the probability of answering "Always" given not answering "Never" is $30.9\% \div 68.7\% \approx 0.45$ or 45%, which is closest to choice C.
Action: Answer("C")

Thought:
  The probability of a user watching videos Always given they did not answer Never is given by P(Always | Not Never)
  P(Always | Not Never) = P(Always and Not Never) / P(Not Never)
  P(Not Never) = P(Rarely) + P(Often) + P(Always) = $24.3 \% + 13.5 \% + 30.9 \% = 68.7 \%$
  P(Always and Not Never) = P(Always) = $30.9 \%$
  P(Always | Not Never) = P(Always and Not Never) / P(Not Never) = $30.9 \% / 68.7 \% ≈ 0.45$
  The closest value to 0.45 is 0.38.

  The question asks us to determine the probability that a tablet user answered "Always" given that they did not answer "Never".
  We can use Bayes' theorem to find the conditional probability of a user answering "Always" given that they did not answer "Never."
  Let N denote the event of answering Never, and A denote the event of answering Always.
  We want to find P(A|~N), the probability of answering Always given not Never.
  By applying Bayes' theorem, we can calculate P(A|~N) = P(~N|A)*P(A)/P(~N)
  We can compute the probabilities as follows: 
  P(A) = 0.309 (given)
  P(N) = 0.313 (given)
  P(~N) = 1 - P(N) = 1 - 0.313 = 0.687
  P(~N|A) = the probability of not answering Never given that you answered Always is 0 because the Always category does not include Never. Therefore, P(~N|A) = 0.
  Therefore, P(A|~N) = P(~N|A)*P(A)/P(~N) = 0*0.309/0.687 = 0.
  This makes intuitive sense because if someone did not answer "Never," it means they must have answered one of the other response options, and "Always" is not one of these other response options.
  The closest answer to 0 is A: 0.31.

  $x \geq 3$    $\qquad$  Marisa must hire at least 3 junior directors
  $y \geq 1$    $\qquad$  Marisa must hire at least 1 senior director
  $x+y \geq 10$ $\qquad$ Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members.
  The Answer is A: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$

  We can use point-slope form of a line: y - y1 = m(x - x1), where m is the slope and (x1, y1) is a point on the line to find the equation of the line.
  Plugging in m = 1/7, x1 = 0, and y1 = 0 into the equation, we get y = 1/7 x. 
  Now let's test each of the given points on this equation to see which one lies on the line.
  A: (0,7) does not lie on the line, because 7 is not equal to 1/7 * 0.
  B: (1,7) does not lie on the line, because 7 is not equal to 1/7 * 1.
  C: (7,7) does lie on the line, because 7 is equal to 1/7 * 7.
  D: (14,2) does not lie on the line, because 2 is not equal to 1/7 * 14.
  Therefore, the point (7,7) lies on the line.

Topic: Math
Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Thought:
- One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal gives 210 / 50 calories.
- One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal has a size of $\frac{3}{4}$ cup.
- One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 mg of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
- One cup of the mixture has a total of 270 calories.
- Let x be the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup.
- The total number of cups is $\frac{3}{4} + x$.
- The total number of calories from Crunchy Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $210\left(\frac{3}{4}\right)$ and the total number of calories from Super Grain cereal is $240x$.
- Therefore, $210\left(\frac{3}{4}\right) + 240x = 270\cdot 1$.
- Solving for x gives $x = \frac{1}{3}$.
- So, $\frac{1}{3}$ $\operatorname{cup}$ of Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture.
- The answer is C: $\frac{1}{3}$ $\operatorname{cup}$.

$$

So, 1 cup of Crunchy Grain Cereal will provide $280=\frac{210}{(\frac {3}{4})}$ cal.

Therefore, let x be the amount of Super Grain cereal in 1 cup of mixture, and (1-x) be the amount of Crunchy Grain cereal in 1 cup of mixture.
In 1 cup of mixture, the total calories from the Super Grain and the Crunchy Grain cereals should add to 270.
Thus, $(240)(x)+(280)(1-x)= 270$
Therefore, solving for x:
    $$ (240)(x)+(280)(1-x)= 270$$
    
   $$\implies240 x + 280 - 280 x = 270$$
   
  $$ \implies -40 x= -10$$
   
   $$\implies x= \frac{1}{4}\operatorname{cup}$$

Thus, $\frac{1}{4}$ of a cup of Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture.
Answer: Answer("B")

  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$

$$

$$

The given equation $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$ represents the height h of the ball t seconds after it is thrown upward with an initial speed of v feet per second from a height of k feet.
We need to find the expression for v in terms of h, t, and k.

Solution:
We can solve the given equation for v and get the expression for v in terms of h, t, and k.
$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$
Moving constants to the right side: 
$v t=h+k-16 t^{2}$ 
Taking $v$ common on the left side: 
$v=t\left(-16 t+\frac{h}{t}+\frac{k}{t}\right)$

$v=-16 t^{2}+h t^{-1}+k t^{-1}$ 
$v=-16 t^{2}+\frac{h+k}{t}$ 

Thus, the expression for $v$ in terms of $h$, $t$, and $k$ is option C:
$v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$.

  - A: $y=-\frac32x+3$
  - B: $y=-\frac34x+\frac32$
  - C: $y=-\frac12x+3$

The line with slope $-\frac34$ is not perpendicular either as the product of the two slopes won't be -1. By comparing the slopes of the last remaining choices, it is evident that the slope of the line in choice A is equal to $-\frac32$. Therefore, the graph of equation $3x+2y=6$ is perpendicular to the graph of the given equation $-2x+3y=6$.
  
  The answer is A: $3 x+2 y=6$.

Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The DBA plans to increase its membership by $n$ businesses every year.
  There were $b$ businesses at the beginning of the year.
  After $1$ year the total number of businesses will be $b+n$.
  After $2$ years the total number of businesses will be $b+2n$.
  After $x$ years, the total number of businesses will be $b+n x$.
  Therefore, $y=n x+b$ is the function that best models the total number of businesses the DBA plans to have as members x years from now.
  The answer is A: $y=n x+b$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
   The number of businesses the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now will increase by the same amount, $n$, per year.
   Therefore, $n$ represents the slope of the function and $b$ represents the initial value.
   The function that models the total number of businesses,
   should be a linear function with an initial value of $b$, and a slope of $n$.
   Therefore, the best choice is A.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
  At the beginning of the year, there were b businesses in the DBA.
  If the DBA wants to increase its membership by n businesses per year, there would be nx businesses increase in n years . 
  We add nx to b to get the total number of businesses.
  Therefore, the function that models it is $y=n x+b$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 3:

  We can use the equation for linear regression $y=mx+b$ to model the situation, where $y$ is the total number of businesses, $x$ is the number of years, $m$ is the slope of the function, and $b$ is the initial number of businesses.
  The slope of the linear function is the increase in businesses per year, which is equal to $n$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $y=nx+b$.

  Since the membership is increasing linearly every year, the best function model to use is $y = nx+b$. Therefore, the answer is A: $y=n x+b$.

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& k x-3 y=4 \\& 4 x-5 y=7\end{aligned}$$In the system of equations above, $k$ is a constant and $x$ and $y$ are variables. For what value of $k$ will the system of equations have no solution?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{12}{5}$
  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can use the determinant of the matrix, which corresponds to the coefficients of the variables in the equations, to determine if the system has a unique solution.
  If the determinant is zero, then the system has no solution or infinite solutions.
  So, we need to find what value of k makes the determinant zero.
  The determinant is $ad-bc$, where $a=k, b=-3, c=4$ and $d=-5$
  So, $k \times (-5) - (-3) \times 4 = -5k+12$ needs to be equal to zero to have no solution.
  Simplifying, we get $-5k+12=0$ which implies, $k = \frac{12}{5}$
  Therefore, the answer is $\textbf{(A) }\frac{12}{5}$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
Looking at the given system of equations:
$$ \begin{aligned}& k x-3 y=4 \\& 4 x-5 y=7\end{aligned} $$
One way to find the value of $k$ that makes the system of equations have no solution is to observe that the two equations represent two lines in a Cartesian plane with slopes $k/3$ and $4/5$. 

Since they have no solution, the lines will be parallel, meaning that their slopes will be equal; so we have:
$$ \frac{k}{3} = \frac{4}{5} $$

Solving the equation for $k$, we get:
$$ k = \frac{12}{5} $$

Therefore, if $k = \frac{12}{5}$, the system of equations has no solution, i.e. the answer is A.

Topic: Math
Question: If $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$, what is the value of $\frac{b}{a} ?$
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4}$
  C: 2
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ using the given equation $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$ as follows:
  $\frac{2a}{b} = \frac{1}{2}$ can be rewritten as:$a = \frac{b}{4}$
  Therefore, $\frac{b}{a} = \frac{b}{\frac{b}{4}} = 4$
  The answer is D: 4.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Thought:
We are given that $\frac{2a}{b} = \frac{1}{2}$. We need to solve for $\frac{b}{a}$. We can start by isolating $\frac{b}{a}$.

$$
\begin{aligned}
\frac{2a}{b} &= \frac{1}{2} \\
\frac{2a}{b} \cdot \frac{b}{2a} &= \frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{b}{2a} \\
\frac{b}{a} &= \frac{1}{4}
\end{aligned}
$$
Therefore, the answer is $\frac{1}{4}$.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 2:
Thought:

Action: 
  cross-multiplying the equation to get rid of the fraction, we have $2a = \frac{1}{2}b$.
  Multiplying both sides by $\frac{2}{b}$, we have $2a \cdot \frac{2}{b} = \frac{1}{2}b \cdot \frac{2}{b}$.
  Simplifying, we have $4\cdot \frac{a}{b} = 1$.
  Dividing both sides by 4, we have $\frac{a}{b} = \frac{1}{4}$.
  To obtain $\frac{b}{a}$, we need to reciprocate $\frac{a}{b}$,  $\frac{b}{a} = \frac{4}{1}$.
  Therefore, the value of $\frac{b}{a}$ is 4.
  So, the answer is $\textbf{(D)}$ 4.

  $$4a = b$$
  Hence, $$\frac{b}{a} = \frac{4a}{a} = 4.$$
